luqum.tree.Item:\n   265→        has_search_fields = False\n   266→        for node, parents in luqum_traverse(q_tree):\n   267→            if isinstance(node, luqum.tree.SearchField):\n   268→                has_search_fields = True\n   269→                if node.name.lower() in self.field_name_map:\n   270→                    node.name = self.field_name_map[node.name.lower()]\n   271→                if node.name == 'isbn':\n   272→                    isbn_transform(node)\n   273→                if node.name in ('lcc', 'lcc_sort'):\n   274→                    lcc_transform(node)\n   275→                if node.name in ('dcc', 'dcc_sort'):\n   276→                    ddc_transform(node)\n   277→\n   278→        if not has_search_fields:\n   279→            # If there are no search fields, k in self.public_api_params & set(params):\n   289→            values = params[k] if isinstance(params[k], list) else [params[k]]\n   290→            for val in values:\n   291→                if k == 'author':\n   292→                    v = val.strip()\n   293→                    m = re_author_key.search(v)\n   294→                    if m:\n   295→                     f\"(author_name:({v}) OR author_alternative_name:({v}))\"\n   300→                        )\n   301→                elif k == 'isbn':\n   302→                    normalized = q_list.append(f'{k}:({fully_escape_query(val)})')\n   306→\n   307→        return ' AND '.join(q_list)\n   308→\n   309→    def q_to_solr_params(  # noqa: PLR0915, C901\n   310→        self,\n   311→        q: str,\n   312→        solr_fields: set[str],\n   313→        cur_solr_params: list[tuple[str, str]],\n   314→        highlight: bool = False,\n   315→    ) -> list[tuple[str, str]]:\n   316→        new_params: list[tuple[str, str]] = []\n   317→\n   318→        # We need to parse the tree so that it gets transformed using the\n   319→        # special OL query parsing rules (different from default solr!)\n   320→        # See luqum_parser for details.\n   321→        work_q_tree = luqum_parser(q)\n   322→\n   323→        # Removes the work prefix from fields; used as the callable argument for 'luqum_replace_field'\n   324→        def remove_work_prefix(field: str) -> str:\n   325→            return field.partition('.')[2] if field.startswith('work.') else field\n   326→\n   327→        # Removes the indicator prefix from queries with the 'work field' before appending them to parameters.\n   328→        final_work_query = deepcopy(work_q_tree)\n   329→        luqum_replace_field(final_work_query, remove_work_prefix)\n   330→        try:\n   331→            luqum_remove_field(final_work_query, lambda f: f.startswith('edition.'))\n   332→        except EmptyTreeError:\n   333→            # If the whole tree is removed, we should just search for everything\n   334→            final_work_query = luqum_parser('*:*')\n   335→\n   336→        new_params.append(('userWorkQuery', str(final_work_query)))\n   337→\n   338→        # This full work query uses solr-specific syntax to add extra parameters\n   339→        # to the way the search is processed. We are using the edismax parser.\n   340→        # See https://solr.apache.org/guide/8_11/the-extended-dismax-query-parser.html\n   341→        # This is somewhat synonymous to setting defType=edismax in the\n   342→        # query, but much more flexible. We wouldn't be able to do our\n   343→        # complicated parent/child queries with defType!\n   344→\n   345→        full_work_query = '({{!edismax q.op=\"AND\" qf=\"{qf}\" pf=\"{pf}\" bf=\"{bf}\" v={v}}})'.format(\n   346→            # qf: the fields to query un-prefixed parts of the query.\n   347→            # e.g. 'harry potter' becomes\n   348→            # 'text:(harry potter) OR alternative_title:(harry potter)^20 OR ...'\n   349→            qf='text alternative_title^10 author_name^10 chapter^5',\n   350→            # pf: phrase fields. This increases the score of documents that\n   351→            # match the query terms in close proximity to each other.\n   352→            pf='alternative_title^10 author_name^10',\n   353→            # bf (boost factor): boost results based on the value of this\n   354→            # field. I.e. results with more editions get boosted, upto a\n   355→            # max of 100, after which we don't see it as good signal of\n   356→            # quality.\n   357→            bf='min(100,edition_count) min(100,def(readinglog_count,0))',\n   358→            # v: the query to process with the edismax query parser. Note\n   359→            # we are using a solr variable here; this reads the url parameter\n   360→            # arbitrarily called userWorkQuery.\n   361→            v='$userWorkQuery',\n   362→        )\n   363→        ed_q = None\n   364→        full_ed_query = None\n   365→        editions_fq = []\n   366→        if req_context.get().solr_editions and 'editions:[subquery]' in solr_fields:\n   367→            WORK_FIELD_TO_ED_FIELD: dict[str, str | Callable[[str], str]] = {\n   368→                # Internals\n   369→                'edition_key': 'key',\n   370→                'text': 'text',\n   371→                # Display data\n   372→                'title': 'title',\n   373→                'title_suggest': 'title_suggest',\n   374→                'subtitle': 'subtitle',\n   375→                'alternative_title': 'alternative_title',\n   376→                'alternative_subtitle': 'subtitle',\n   377→                'cover_i': 'cover_i',\n   378→                # 'author_alternative_name': 'author_alternative_name',\n   383→                # 'author_facet': 'author_facet',\n   384→                # Misc useful data\n   385→                'format': 'format',\n   386→                'language': 'language',\n   387→                'chapter': 'chapter',\n   388→                'publisher': 'publisher',\n   389→                'publisher_facet': 'publisher_facet',\n   390→                'publish_date': 'publish_date',\n   391→                'publish_year': 'publish_year',\n   392→                # Mainly involves removing\n   425→                invalid fields, or renaming fields as necessary.\n   426→                \"\"\"\n   427→                q_tree = luqum_parser(work_query)\n   428→                for node, parents in luqum_traverse(q_tree):\n   429→                    if isinstance(node, luqum.tree.SearchField) and node.name != '*':\n   430→                        if node.name.startswith('edition.'):\n   431→                            ed_field = node.name.partition('.')[2]\n   432→                        else:\n   433→                            ed_field = node.name\n   434→\n   435→                        new_name = convert_work_field_to_edition_field(ed_field)\n   436→                        if new_name is None:\n   437→                            try:\n   438→                                luqum_remove_child(node, parents)\n   439→                            except EmptyTreeError:\n   440→                                # Deleted the whole tree! Nothing left\n   441→                                return ''\n   442→                        elif isinstance(new_name, str):\n   443→                            parent = parents[-1] if parents else None\n   444→                            # Prefixing with + makes the field mandatory\n   445→                            if isinstance(\n   446→                                parent,\n   447→                                (\n   448→                                    luqum.tree.Not,\n   449→                                    luqum.tree.Prohibit,\n   450→                                    luqum.tree.OrOperation,\n   451→                                ),\n   452→                            ):\n   453→                                node.name = new_name\n   454→                            else:\n   455→                                node.name = f'+{new_name}'\n   456→                            if new_name == 'key':\n   457→                                # need to convert eg 'edition_key:OL123M' to\n   458→                                # 'key:(/books/OL123M)'. Shouldn't happen\n   488→                            raise ValueError(f'Invalid new_name: {new_name}')\n   489→                return str(q_tree)\n   490→\n   491→            # Move over all fq parameters that can be applied to editions.\n   492→            # These are generally used to handle facets.\n   493→            editions_fq = ['type:edition']\n   494→            for param_name, param_value in cur_solr_params:\n   495→                if param_name != 'fq' or param_value.startswith('type:'):\n   496→                    continue\n   497→                field_name, field_val = param_value.split(':', 1)\n   498→                if ed_field := convert_work_field_to_edition_field(field_name):\n   499→                    editions_fq.append(f'{ed_field}:{field_val}')\n   500→            for fq in editions_fq:\n   501→                new_params.append(('editions.fq', fq))\n   502→\n   503→            user_lang = convert_iso_to_marc(self.lang) or 'eng'\n   504→\n   505→            ed_q = convert_work_query_to_edition_query(str(work_q_tree))\n   506→            #            # bq (boost query): Boost which edition is promoted to the top\n   525→                bq=' '.join(\n   526→                    (\n   527→ 591→                }\n   592→            # The elements in _this_ edition query will match but not affect\n   593→            # whether the work appears in search results\n   594→            new_params.append(\n   595→                (\n   596→                    'editions.q',\n   597→                    # Here we use the special terms parser to only filter the\n   598→                    # editions for a given, already matching work '_root_' node.\n   599→                    f'({{!terms f=_root_ v=$row.key}}) AND {full_ed_query}',\n   600→                )\n   601→            )\n   602→            new_params.append(('editions.rows', '1'))\n   603→            new_params.append(('editions.fl', ','.join(edition_fields)))\n   604→        return new_params\n   605→\n   606→    def add_non_solr_fields(\n   607→        self,\n   608→        non_solr_fields: set[str],\n   609→        solr_result: dict,\n   610→    ) -> None:\n   611→        from openlibrary.plugins.upstream.models import Edition, Work\n   612→\n   613→        prefixed_fields = {\n   614→            prefixed_field\n   615→            for field in non_solr_fields\n   616→            for prefixed_field in (\n   617→                (field,) if '.' in field else (f'work.{field}', f'editions.{field}')\n   618→            )\n   619→        }\n   620→        need_works = any(field.startswith('work.') for field in Note that if there is no edition query (because no fields in\n            # the user's work query apply), we use the special value *:* to\n            # match everything, but still get boosting.\n            new_params.append(('userEdQuery', ed_q or '*:*'))\n            # need to specify it twice.\n            new_params.append(('editions.userEdQuery', ed_q or '*:*'))\n            new_params.append(('editions.ol.label', 'EDITION_MATCH'))\n\n            full_ed_query = '({{!edismax bq=\"{bq}\" v={v} qf=\"{qf}\"}})'.format(\n                # See qf in work_query\n                qf='text alternative_title^4 author_name^4 chapter^4',\n                # Reading from the url parameter userEdQuery. This lets us avoid\n                # having to try to escape the query in order to fit inside this\n                # other query.\n                v='$userEdQuery',\n                # bq (boost query): Boost which edition is promoted to the top\n                bq=' '.join(\n                    (\n                        f'language:{user_lang}^40',\n                        'ebook_access:public^10',\n                        'ebook_access:borrowable^8',\n                        'ebook_access:printdisabled^2',\n                        'cover_i:*^2',\n                    )\n                ),\n            )\n\n        if ed_q or len(editions_fq) > 1:\n            # The elements in _this_ edition query should cause works not to\n            # match _at all_ if matching editions are not found\n            new_params.append(\n                ('fullEdQuery', cast(str, full_ed_query) if ed_q else '*:*')\n            )\n            q = (\n                f'+{full_work_query} '\n                # This is using the special parent query syntax to, on top of\n                # the user's `full_work_query`, also only find works which have\n                # editions matching the edition query.\n                # Also include edition-less works (i.e. edition_count:0)\n                '+('\n                '_query_:\"{!parent which=type:work v=$fullEdQuery filters=$editions.fq}\" '\n                'OR edition_count:0'\n                ')'\n            )\n            new_params.append(('q', q))\n        else:\n            new_params.append(('q', full_work_query))\n\n        if highlight:\n            highlight_fields = ('subject', 'chapter')\n            try:\n                # This can throw the EmptyTreeError if nothing remains in the query\n                highlight_query = luqum_deepcopy(work_q_tree)\n                luqum_remove_field(\n                    highlight_query,\n                    lambda f: f not in highlight_fields,\n                )\n                new_params.append(('hl', 'true'))\n                # NOTE: This only applies to the work, really\n                new_params.append(('hl.fl', ','.join(highlight_fields)))\n                new_params.append(('hl.q', str(highlight_query)))\n                new_params.append(('hl.snippets', '10'))\n                # we can't trim e.g. chapter since it has a specific structure with the pipes\n                new_params.append(('hl.fragsize', '0'))\n            except EmptyTreeError:\n                # nothing to highlight\n                pass\n\n        if full_ed_query:\n            edition_fields = {\n                f.split('.', 1)[1] for f in solr_fields if f.startswith('editions.')\n            }\n            if not edition_fields:\n                edition_fields = solr_fields - {\n                    # Default to same fields as for the work...\n                    'editions:[subquery]',\n                    # but exclude the author fields since they're primarily work data;\n                    # they only exist on editions to improve search matches.\n                    'author_name',\n                    'author_key',\n                    'author_alternative_name',\n                    'author_facet',\n                }\n            # The elements in _this_ edition query will match but not affect\n            # whether the work appears in search results\n            new_params.append(\n                (\n                    'editions.q',\n                    # Here we use the special terms parser to only filter the\n                    # editions for a given, already matching work '_root_' node.\n                    f'({{!terms f=_root_ v=$row.key}}) AND {full_ed_query}',\n                )\n            )\n            new_params.append(('editions.rows', '1'))\n            new_params.append(('editions.fl', ','.join(edition_fields)))\n        return new_params\n\n    def add_non_solr_fields(\n        self,\n        non_solr_fields: set[str],\n        solr_result: dict,\n    ) -> None:\n        from openlibrary.plugins.upstream.models import Edition, Work\n\n        prefixed_fields = {\n            prefixed_field\n            for field in non_solr_fields\n            for prefixed_field in (\n                (field,) if '.' in field else (f'work.{field}', f'editions.{field}')\n            )\n        }\n        need_works = any(field.startswith('work.') for field in prefixed_fields)\n        need_editions = any(field.startswith('editions.') for field in prefixed_fields)\n\n        # Could be `None` if the record has been deleted and Solr not yet updated.\n                    if not db_thing:\n                        continue\n\n                    val = getattr(db_thing, field_name)\n                    if field_name == 'providers':\n                        ed = cast(Edition, db_thing)\n                        solr_doc[field_name] = [\n                            acq.__dict__ for acq in get_acquisitions(solr_doc, ed)\n                        ]\n                    elif isinstance(val, infogami.infobase.client.Nothing):\n                        continue\n                    elif field_name == 'description':\n                        solr_doc[field_name] = (\n                            val if isinstance(val, str) else val.value\n                        )\n\n\ndef lcc_transform(sf: luqum.tree.SearchField):\n    # e.g. lcc:[NC1 TO NC1000] to lcc:[NC-0001.00000000 TO NC-1000.00000000]\n    # for proper range search\n    val = sf.children[0]\n    if isinstance(val, luqum.tree.Range):\n        normed_range = normalize_lcc_range(val.low.value, val.high.value)\n        if normed_range:\n            val.low.value, val.high.value = normed_range\n    elif isinstance(val, luqum.tree.Word):\n        if '*' in val.value and not val.value.startswith('*'):\n            # Marshals human repr into solr repr\n            # lcc:A720* should become A--0720*\n            parts = val.value.split('*', 1)\n            lcc_prefix = normalize_lcc_prefix(parts[0])\n            val.value = (lcc_prefix or parts[0]) + '*' + parts[1]\n        else:\n            normed = short_lcc_to_sortable_lcc(val.value.strip('\"'))\n            if normed:\n                val.value = normed\n    elif isinstance(val, luqum.tree.Phrase):\n        normed = short_lcc_to_sortable_lcc(val.value.strip('\"'))\n        if normed:\n            val.value = f'\"{normed}\"'\n    elif (\n        isinstance(val, luqum.tree.Group)\n        and isinstance(val.expr, luqum.tree.UnknownOperation)\n        and all(isinstance(c, luqum.tree.Word) for c in val.expr.children)\n    ):\n        # Set of queries that define the universe of this scheme\n    universe: frozenset[str]\n    # All actual solr fields that can be in a user query\n    all_fields: frozenset[str]\n    # Fields that can be read, but which aren't stored in solr\n    non_solr_fields: frozenset[str]\n    # Allow custom randoms; so anything random_* is allowed\n                # Also Allow custom time randoms to allow carousels with overlapping\n                # books to have a fresh ordering when on the same collection\n                sort_order: str | None = None\n                if ' ' in sort:\n                    sort, sort_order = sort.split(' ', 1)\n                random_type, random_seed = sort.split('_', 1)\n                solr_sort = self.sorts[random_type]\n                solr_sort_str = solr_sort() if callable(solr_sort) else solr_sort\n                solr_sort_field, solr_sort_order = solr_sort_str.split(' ', 1)\n                sort_order = sort_order or solr_sort_order\n                return f'{solr_sort_field}_{random_seed} {sort_order}'\n            else:\n                solr_sort = self.sorts[sort]\n                return solr_sort() if callable(solr_sort) else solr_sort\n\n        return ','.join(\n            process_individual_sort(s.strip()) for s in user_sort.split(',')\n        )\n\n    def process_user_query(self, q_param: str) -> str:\n        if q_param == '*:*':\n            #
